### <a id="the-inductive-types-h-s-p-v">The Inductive Types H, S, P, V</a>

This section presents the [Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="329" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="333" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="341" class="Pragma">--without-K</a> <a id="353" class="Pragma">--exact-split</a> <a id="367" class="Pragma">--safe</a> <a id="374" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

<a id="379" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="384" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="391" href="Algebras.Signatures.html" class="Module">Algebras.Signatures</a> <a id="411" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="418" href="Algebras.Signatures.html#1299" class="Function">Signature</a><a id="427" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="429" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5723" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a><a id="430" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="432" href="Universes.html#262" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="433" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="435" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="440" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="447" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html" class="Module">MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems</a> <a id="473" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="479" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="480" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="494" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="497" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="504" href="Varieties.Varieties.html" class="Module">Varieties.Varieties</a> <a id="524" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="525" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a> <a id="527" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="529" href="Algebras.Signatures.html#1299" class="Function">Signature</a> <a id="539" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5723" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a> <a id="541" href="Universes.html#262" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="542" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="544" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#544" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="548" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="550" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="564" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="566" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="573" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="578" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="585" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html" class="Module">Varieties.EquationalLogic</a><a id="610" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="611" class="Argument">𝑆</a> <a id="613" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="615" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="616" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="618" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#544" class="Bound">gfe</a><a id="621" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="623" class="Keyword">public</a>
<a id="630" class="Comment">--open import MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems using (hfunext) -- public</a>

</pre>


Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`). The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

A **variety** is a class of algebras, in the same signature, that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images, subalgebras, and arbitrary products.  To represent varieties we define inductive types for the closure operators `H`, `S`, and `P` that are composable.  Separately, we define an inductive type `V` which simultaneously represents closure under all three operators, `H`, `S`, and `P`.




#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphic closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

</pre>



#### <a id="subalgebraic-closure">Subalgebraic closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of a class of algebras that is closed under the taking of subalgebras is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

</pre>



#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of an class of algebras closed under the taking of arbitrary products is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3624" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="3629" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="3631" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3632" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4131" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4133" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4134" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4135" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4136" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4138" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4139" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4141" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3648" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4143" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4145" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4093" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4147" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4149" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4110" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4151" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4153" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4110" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4155" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4157" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4159" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3648" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="P.pisow"></a><a id="4162" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4162" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a>  <a id="4169" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4171" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4172" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4172" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4174" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4174" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4176" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4178" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4186" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4188" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4189" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4191" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4193" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4172" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4195" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4197" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4198" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4199" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4200" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4202" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3634" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4203" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4205" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3648" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4207" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4209" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4172" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4211" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4213" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4174" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4215" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4217" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4174" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4219" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4221" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4223" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3648" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="varietal-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will denote it by `V`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="4563" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="4568" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="4570" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4571" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4573" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4573" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4575" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4577" href="Universes.html#205" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="4585" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="4587" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4589" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4591" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="4595" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4596" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4604" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4606" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4607" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="4609" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4631" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4633" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4635" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5222" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5224" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="5226" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5173" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5228" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5230" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5232" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="V.visou"></a><a id="5235" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5235" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a>  <a id="5242" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5244" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5245" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5245" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5247" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5249" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5257" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5259" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5260" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5262" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5262" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5264" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5266" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5274" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5276" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5277" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5279" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5281" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5245" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5283" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5285" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5286" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5287" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5288" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5290" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5291" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5293" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5295" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5297" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5245" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5299" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5301" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5262" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5303" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5305" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5262" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5307" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5309" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5311" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="V.visow"></a><a id="5314" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a>  <a id="5321" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5323" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5324" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5324" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5326" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5326" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5328" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5330" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5338" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5340" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5341" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5343" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5345" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5324" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5347" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5349" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5350" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5351" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5352" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5354" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4573" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5355" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5357" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5359" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5361" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5324" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5363" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5365" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5326" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5367" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5369" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5326" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5371" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5373" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5375" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

With the closure operator V representing closure under HSP, we represent formally what it means to be a variety of algebras as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="is-variety"></a><a id="5727" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5727" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5738" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5740" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5741" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5741" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5743" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5745" href="Universes.html#205" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="5753" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5755" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5755" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5757" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5759" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5764" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5765" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5773" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5741" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5775" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5776" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5778" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5781" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5741" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5782" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5785" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5787" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5790" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5741" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5792" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5794" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5727" class="Function">is-variety</a><a id="5804" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5805" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5805" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5806" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5808" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5808" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5810" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5812" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5813" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5814" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5805" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5815" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5817" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5805" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5818" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5820" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5808" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5822" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="5824" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5808" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

<a id="variety"></a><a id="5827" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5827" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5835" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5837" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5838" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5838" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5840" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5842" href="Universes.html#205" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="5850" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5852" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5854" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5855" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5858" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5838" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5859" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="5860" href="Universes.html#181" class="Function Operator">⁺</a> <a id="5862" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5864" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5827" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5872" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5872" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5874" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5876" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="5878" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5878" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5880" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="5882" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5883" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5888" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5889" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5897" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5872" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5899" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5900" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5902" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5905" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5872" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5906" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5909" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="5911" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5727" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5922" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5878" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="V-is-closed-under-lift">V is closed under lift</a>

As mentioned earlier, a technical hurdle that must be overcome when formalizing proofs in Agda is the proper handling of universe levels. In particular, in the proof of the Birkhoff's theorem, for example, we will need to know that if an algebra 𝑨 belongs to the variety V 𝒦, then so does the lift of 𝑨.  Let us get the tedious proof of this technical lemma out of the way.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="6391" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="6396" href="Prelude.Lifts.html#2674" class="Module">Lift</a>
<a id="6401" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="6408" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6408" class="Module">_</a> <a id="6410" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6411" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6413" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6415" href="Universes.html#205" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="6423" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6425" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6425" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6427" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6429" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6434" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6435" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6443" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6445" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6446" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6448" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6451" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6452" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="6455" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="6463" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="6467" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6469" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6470" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6470" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6472" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6474" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6482" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6483" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6486" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6487" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6489" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6490" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6492" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6494" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6470" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6496" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="6498" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="6499" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6500" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6501" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6503" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6506" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6507" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6509" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6425" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
       <a id="6518" class="Comment">------------------------------------------</a>
  <a id="6563" class="Symbol">→</a>    <a id="6568" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4658" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="6577" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6470" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6579" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6580" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6583" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6585" href="Universes.html#181" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="6586" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6588" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="6590" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="6591" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6592" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6593" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6595" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6598" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6600" href="Universes.html#181" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="6601" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6603" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6425" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="7772" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="7776" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7777" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5235" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a><a id="7782" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7783" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7783" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7784" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7786" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7786" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7787" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7789" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7789" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7791" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7791" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7794" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7796" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7798" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="7804" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7805" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4716" class="InductiveConstructor">vlift</a> <a id="7811" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7789" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7812" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7814" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7815" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3489" class="Function">lift-alg-iso</a> <a id="7828" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7791" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7831" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="7834" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="7838" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7839" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a><a id="7844" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7845" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7845" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7846" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7848" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7848" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7849" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7851" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7851" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7853" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7853" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7856" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7858" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7860" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="7866" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7867" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="7871" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7851" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7872" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7874" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7875" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3489" class="Function">lift-alg-iso</a> <a id="7888" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7853" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7891" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties that we need later.

First, `P` is a closure operator.  This is proved by checking that `P` is *monotone*, *expansive*, and *idempotent*. The meaning of these terms will be clear from the definitions of the types that follow.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="9068" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8966" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9076" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9077" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3720" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a> <a id="9083" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9083" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9084" class="Symbol">)</a>    <a id="9089" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9091" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3842" class="InductiveConstructor">pliftw</a> <a id="9098" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9083" class="Bound">x</a>

 <a id="9239" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8966" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9247" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9248" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4001" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a> <a id="9254" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9254" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9255" class="Symbol">)</a>    <a id="9260" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9262" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4001" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a> <a id="9268" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="9271" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9271" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="9273" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9275" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8966" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9283" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9284" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9254" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9286" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9271" class="Bound">i</a><a id="9287" class="Symbol">))</a>

 <a id="9336" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8966" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9344" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9345" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4162" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="9351" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9351" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9353" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9353" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="9355" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9357" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9359" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4162" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="9365" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9366" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8966" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9374" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9351" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9375" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9377" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9353" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

Similarly, S is a closure operator.  The facts that S is idempotent and expansive won't be needed below, so we omit these, but we will make use of monotonicity of S.  Here is the proof of the latter.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="S-mono"></a><a id="9608" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9608" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9615" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9617" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9618" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9618" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9620" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9620" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="9622" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9624" href="Universes.html#205" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="9632" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9634" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9634" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9636" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9636" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="9639" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9641" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="9646" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9647" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="9655" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9618" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9657" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="9658" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="9660" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="9663" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9618" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9664" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="9668" class="Symbol">→</a>       <a id="9676" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9634" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9678" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="9680" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9636" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="9683" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9685" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="9686" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9687" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9618" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9688" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9690" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9620" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9691" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9693" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9634" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9695" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="9697" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="9698" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9699" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9618" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9700" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9702" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9620" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9703" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9705" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9636" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a>

<a id="9709" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9608" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9716" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9716" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9720" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9721" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="9727" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9727" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9728" class="Symbol">)</a>            <a id="9741" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9743" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="9749" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9750" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9716" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9754" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9727" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9755" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="9757" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9608" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9764" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9764" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9768" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9769" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3087" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="9774" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9775" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9775" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="9776" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9778" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9778" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9779" class="Symbol">)</a>         <a id="9789" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9791" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3087" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a> <a id="9797" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9798" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9608" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9805" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9764" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9809" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9778" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9810" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="9812" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9608" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9819" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9819" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9823" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9824" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3151" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="9828" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9829" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9829" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="9830" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9832" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9832" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="9833" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9835" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9835" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="9838" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9838" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="9841" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="9844" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9846" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3151" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a> <a id="9851" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9852" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9608" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9859" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9819" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9863" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9835" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="9865" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9867" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9838" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="9871" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9608" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9878" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9878" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9882" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9883" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3229" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="9888" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9889" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9889" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="9890" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9892" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9892" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="9893" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9895" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9895" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="9898" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9898" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="9901" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9903" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9905" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3229" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="9911" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9912" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9608" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9919" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9878" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9923" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9895" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="9925" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9927" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9898" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="9931" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9608" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9938" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9938" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9942" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9943" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3292" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="9948" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9948" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9950" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9950" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="9952" class="Symbol">)</a>          <a id="9963" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9965" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3292" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="9970" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9971" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9608" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9978" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9938" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9982" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9948" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9983" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9985" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9950" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="10197" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="10204" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10204" class="Module">_</a> <a id="10206" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10207" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10207" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10209" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10209" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="10211" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10213" href="Universes.html#205" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="10221" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10223" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10223" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10225" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10227" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="10232" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10233" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10241" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10207" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10243" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10244" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="10246" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10249" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10207" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10250" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="10253" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="10261" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10261" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="10274" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10276" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10277" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10277" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10279" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10281" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10289" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10290" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10207" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10292" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="10294" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10209" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="10295" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10297" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10298" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10300" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10302" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10277" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10304" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#5248" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10324" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10223" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10326" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10328" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10277" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10330" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="10332" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="10333" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10334" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10207" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10335" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10337" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10209" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="10338" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10340" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10223" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="10344" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10261" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="10357" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10358" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10358" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="10359" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10361" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10362" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10362" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10364" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10366" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10368" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10368" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="10370" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10372" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10372" class="Bound">C≤A</a><a id="10375" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10377" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10379" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10379" class="Bound">KA</a> <a id="10382" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10384" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10384" class="Bound">B≅C</a><a id="10387" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="10390" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10392" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3151" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a> <a id="10397" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10511" class="Function">sA</a> <a id="10400" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10415" class="Function">B≤A</a>

 <a id="10710" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10631" class="Function">S→subalgebra</a> <a id="10723" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10724" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="10729" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10730" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10730" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="10731" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10733" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10733" class="Bound">x</a><a id="10734" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10736" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10738" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10730" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10740" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10742" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10743" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10730" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10745" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10747" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#6572" class="Function">≤-refl</a><a id="10753" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10755" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10757" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10733" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="10759" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10761" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10762" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1648" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="10768" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2841" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="10778" class="Symbol">)</a>

   <a id="11835" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#11835" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="11838" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11840" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#1333" class="Function">Subalgebra</a> <a id="11851" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13786" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="11853" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#11779" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="11856" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13786" class="Function Operator">∣</a>
   <a id="11861" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#11835" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="11864" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11866" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13790" class="Function">fst</a> <a id="11870" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13864" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="11872" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#11779" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="11875" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13864" class="Function Operator">∥</a>
   <a id="11880" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#11880" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="11885" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11887" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#11696" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="11889" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="11891" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13786" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="11893" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#11835" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="11896" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13786" class="Function Operator">∣</a>
   <a id="11901" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#11880" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="11906" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11908" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13868" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="11912" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13864" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="11914" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13868" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="11918" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#11779" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="11921" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13864" class="Function Operator">∥</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">
<a id="12204" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="12211" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12211" class="Module">_</a> <a id="12213" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12214" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12214" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="12216" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12216" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="12218" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12220" href="Universes.html#205" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="12228" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12230" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12230" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="12232" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12234" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="12239" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12240" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="12248" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12214" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="12250" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="12251" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="12253" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="12256" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12214" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="12257" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="12260" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="12304" class="Symbol">→</a>              <a id="12319" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12285" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="12321" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#5248" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="12341" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12342" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="12343" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12344" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12214" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="12345" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12347" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12214" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="12348" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12350" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12230" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="12351" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="12486" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12268" class="Function">lift-alg-subP</a> <a id="12500" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12501" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12501" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="12502" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="12504" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12504" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="12506" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12508" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12509" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12509" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="12511" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12513" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12513" class="Bound">C≤A</a><a id="12516" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12518" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12520" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12520" class="Bound">pA</a> <a id="12523" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12525" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12525" class="Bound">B≅C</a> <a id="12529" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12531" class="Symbol">=</a>

The next lemma would be too obvious to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

<pre class="Agda">

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the main objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

<pre class="Agda">
<a id="14376" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="14383" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14383" class="Module">_</a> <a id="14385" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14386" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14386" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14388" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14388" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="14390" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14392" href="Universes.html#205" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="14400" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14402" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14402" class="Bound">fe</a> <a id="14405" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14407" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="14415" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14388" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="14417" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14386" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14418" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14420" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14420" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="14422" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14424" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="14428" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14429" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="14437" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14386" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14439" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="14440" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14442" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14445" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14386" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14446" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="14449" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="14457" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14457" class="Function">lemPS⊆SP</a> <a id="14466" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14468" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14469" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14469" class="Bound">I</a> <a id="14471" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14473" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14388" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="14475" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="14476" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14478" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14478" class="Bound">ℬ</a> <a id="14480" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14482" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14469" class="Bound">I</a> <a id="14484" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14486" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="14494" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14386" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14496" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="14497" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="14501" class="Symbol">→</a>         <a id="14511" class="Symbol">(∀</a> <a id="14514" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14514" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14516" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14518" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14519" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14478" class="Bound">ℬ</a> <a id="14521" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14514" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14522" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14524" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#5248" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="14544" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14420" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="14545" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="15237" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15237" class="Function">⨅SA≤⨅𝒜</a> <a id="15244" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15246" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="15248" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14762" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="15251" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#4257" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="15253" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="15255" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14717" class="Function">𝒜</a>

  <a id="15283" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15283" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="15285" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15287" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="15289" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14717" class="Function">𝒜</a> <a id="15291" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="15293" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="15295" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14420" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="15299" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15283" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="15301" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15303" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3919" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="15309" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="15312" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15312" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15314" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15316" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8775" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="15323" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15324" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13786" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="15326" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13868" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="15330" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13864" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="15332" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14663" class="Bound">B≤K</a> <a id="15336" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15312" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15338" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13864" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="15340" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13786" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="15341" class="Symbol">))</a>


</pre>



#### <a id="PS-in-SP">PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

  <a id="16576" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="16585" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16585" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="16587" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16589" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16590" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16590" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="16592" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16594" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16527" class="Bound">I</a><a id="16595" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16597" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16599" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16600" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16530" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="16602" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16590" class="Bound">i</a><a id="16603" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16605" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#5248" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="16625" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16626" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="16627" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16628" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15567" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16629" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16631" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16634" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15567" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16635" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16637" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15581" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="16638" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="16643" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16585" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="16645" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16645" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="16647" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16649" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10631" class="Function">S→subalgebra</a> <a id="16662" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16663" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15619" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="16669" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16516" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="16673" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16674" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16533" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16676" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16645" class="Bound">i</a><a id="16677" class="Symbol">))</a>

   <a id="16684" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16684" class="Function">η</a> <a id="16686" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16688" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="16690" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16530" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="16692" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#5248" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="16712" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16713" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="16714" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16715" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16718" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15567" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16719" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16721" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16724" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15567" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16725" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16727" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16728" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="16729" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16730" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15567" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16731" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16733" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16736" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15567" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16737" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16739" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15581" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="16740" class="Symbol">))</a>
   <a id="16746" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16684" class="Function">η</a> <a id="16748" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16750" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14457" class="Function">lemPS⊆SP</a> <a id="16759" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16760" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16763" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15567" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16764" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16766" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16767" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16770" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15567" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16771" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16773" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16774" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16516" class="Bound">hfe</a><a id="16777" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16779" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16780" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="16782" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15581" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="16783" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16785" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16786" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16527" class="Bound">I</a><a id="16787" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16789" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16790" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16530" class="Bound">𝒜</a><a id="16791" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16793" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16585" class="Function">ξ</a>

 <a id="16797" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15619" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="16803" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16803" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="16807" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16808" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4083" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a><a id="16813" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16814" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16814" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="16815" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16817" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16817" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="16818" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16820" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16820" class="Bound">pA</a> <a id="16823" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16823" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="16826" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16828" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16830" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3292" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="16835" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16836" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15619" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="16842" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16803" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="16846" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16820" class="Bound">pA</a><a id="16848" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16850" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16823" class="Bound">A≅B</a>
 <a id="16855" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15619" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="16861" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16861" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="16865" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16866" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4162" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a><a id="16871" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16872" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16872" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="16873" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16875" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16875" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="16876" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16878" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16878" class="Bound">pA</a> <a id="16881" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16881" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="16884" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16886" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16888" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3292" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="16893" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16894" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15619" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="16900" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16861" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="16904" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16878" class="Bound">pA</a><a id="16906" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16908" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16881" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this subsection with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play later (e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem).

<a id="17596" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17500" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17601" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17602" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="17607" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17608" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17608" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17609" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17611" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17611" class="Bound">PCloA</a><a id="17616" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17618" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17620" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17158" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="17624" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17625" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4162" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="17631" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17611" class="Bound">PCloA</a> <a id="17637" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2841" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="17647" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="17685" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17500" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17690" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17691" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3151" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="17695" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17696" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17696" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17697" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17699" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17699" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="17700" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17702" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17702" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="17706" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17706" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="17709" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17711" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17713" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5009" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="17720" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17721" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17500" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17726" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17702" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="17729" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17731" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17706" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="17735" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17500" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17740" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17741" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3229" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="17746" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17747" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17747" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17748" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17750" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17750" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="17751" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17753" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17753" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="17757" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17757" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="17760" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17762" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17764" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5009" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="17771" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17772" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17500" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17777" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17753" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="17780" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17782" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17757" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="17786" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17500" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17791" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17792" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3292" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="17797" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17797" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17799" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17799" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="17801" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17803" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17805" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="17811" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17812" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17500" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17817" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17797" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17818" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17820" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17799" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We just proved that `SP(𝒦) ⊆ V(𝒦)`, and we did so under fairly general assumptions about the universe level parameters.  Unfortunately, this is sometimes not quite general enough, so we now prove the inclusion again for the specific universe parameters that align with subsequent applications of this result.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="18160" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="18167" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18167" class="Module">_</a> <a id="18169" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18170" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18170" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18172" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18174" href="Universes.html#205" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="18182" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18184" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18184" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18186" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18188" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18193" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18194" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18202" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18170" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18204" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18205" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18207" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18208" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18211" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18170" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18212" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="18215" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="18223" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18223" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18229" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18231" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="18232" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18233" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18236" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18170" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18237" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18239" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18242" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18170" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18244" href="Universes.html#181" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18245" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18247" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18248" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="18249" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18250" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18170" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18251" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18253" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18256" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18170" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18257" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18259" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18184" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18260" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18262" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="18264" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="18266" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18184" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="18270" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18223" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18276" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18277" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="18282" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18283" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18283" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18284" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18286" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18286" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18287" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18289" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18291" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="18297" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18298" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18302" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18303" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17500" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18308" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18309" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="18315" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18286" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18316" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="18320" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18321" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1648" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="18327" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18328" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4164" class="Function">lift-alg-associative</a> <a id="18349" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18283" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18350" class="Symbol">))</a>
 <a id="18354" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18223" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18360" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18361" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3087" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a> <a id="18367" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18367" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18368" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18370" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18372" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18376" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18377" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17500" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18382" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18367" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18383" class="Symbol">)</a>
