  <a id="18447" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="18456" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18456" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="18461" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18463" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18402" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="18465" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#4257" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="18467" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4658" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="18476" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18399" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18478" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18479" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18482" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18170" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18484" href="Universes.html#181" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18485" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="18490" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18456" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="18495" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18497" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#8660" class="Function">≤-lift-alg</a> <a id="18508" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18399" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18510" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18409" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

 <a id="18516" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18223" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18522" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18523" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3229" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="18529" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18529" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="18533" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18533" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="18536" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18538" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18540" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5009" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="18547" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18548" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18223" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18554" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18529" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="18557" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18559" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18533" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

 <a id="18565" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18223" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18571" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18572" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3292" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a><a id="18576" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18577" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18577" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18578" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18580" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18580" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="18581" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18583" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18583" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18585" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18585" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="18588" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18590" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18592" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="18598" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18599" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18603" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18604" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17500" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18609" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18583" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18610" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18613" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18626" class="Function">γ</a>
  <a id="18617" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="18626" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18626" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="18628" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18630" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4658" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="18639" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18577" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18641" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18642" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18645" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18170" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18647" href="Universes.html#181" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18648" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18650" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="18652" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18580" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
   <a id="18657" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18626" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="18659" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18661" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1826" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="18669" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18670" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1648" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="18676" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2841" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="18686" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18688" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18585" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="S-in-SP">⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we prove a result that plays an important role, e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem. As we saw in [Algebras.Products][], the (informal) product `⨅ S(𝒦)` of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally) in the [UALib][] as `⨅ 𝔄 S(𝒦)`. Our goal is to prove that this product belongs to `SP(𝒦)`. We do so by first proving that the product belongs to `PS(𝒦)` and then applying the `PS⊆SP` lemma.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="19188" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="19195" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19195" class="Module">_</a> <a id="19197" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19198" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19198" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19200" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19202" href="Universes.html#205" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="19210" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19212" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19212" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="19214" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19216" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19198" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19218" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="19219" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19221" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19221" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19223" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19225" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19230" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19231" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19239" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19198" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19241" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19242" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19244" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19247" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19198" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19248" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19251" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="19259" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19259" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="19277" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19279" href="Algebras.Products.html#4222" class="Function">class-product</a><a id="19292" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19293" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19198" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19294" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19296" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19198" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19297" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19299" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19212" class="Bound">X</a><a id="19300" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="19302" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19304" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19221" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19305" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19307" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19309" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="19310" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19311" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19314" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19198" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19315" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19317" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19320" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19198" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19321" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="19323" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19325" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19221" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19326" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="19330" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19259" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="19348" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19350" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4083" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a> <a id="19356" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19621" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="19363" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19364" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4610" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="19367" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19672" class="Function">llA≅A</a><a id="19372" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="19376" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="19384" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19384" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="19387" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19387" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19391" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19393" href="Algebras.Products.html#2793" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19395" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19396" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19398" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19221" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19399" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19401" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19403" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19411" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19412" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19415" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19198" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19416" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19418" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
  <a id="19422" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19384" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="19425" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19425" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19427" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="19430" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4658" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="19439" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19440" href="Algebras.Products.html#4023" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="19442" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19443" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19445" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19221" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19446" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19448" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19425" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19449" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19451" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19452" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19455" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19198" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19456" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="19460" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19387" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19464" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19464" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19466" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19468" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4658" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="19477" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19478" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19384" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="19481" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19464" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19482" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19484" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19485" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19488" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19198" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19489" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="19494" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19494" class="Function">slA</a> <a id="19498" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19500" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19502" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19502" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19504" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19506" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19507" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19384" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="19510" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19502" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19511" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19513" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19515" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19517" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19221" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="19521" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19494" class="Function">slA</a> <a id="19525" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19525" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19527" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19529" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3292" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="19534" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19535" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13790" class="Function">fst</a> <a id="19539" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13864" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="19541" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19525" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19543" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13864" class="Function Operator">∥</a><a id="19544" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19546" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2841" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a>

  <a id="19560" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Function">psllA</a> <a id="19566" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19568" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19570" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19570" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19572" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19574" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19575" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19387" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19579" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19570" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19580" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19582" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19584" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="19586" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19587" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19589" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19221" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19590" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="19594" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Function">psllA</a> <a id="19600" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19600" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19602" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19604" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3720" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a> <a id="19610" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19611" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19494" class="Function">slA</a> <a id="19615" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19600" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19616" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="19621" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19621" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="19628" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19630" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="19632" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19387" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19636" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19638" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="19640" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19641" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19643" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19221" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19644" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="19648" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19621" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="19655" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19657" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3919" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="19663" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Function">psllA</a>

  <a id="19672" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19672" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="19678" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19680" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19682" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19682" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19684" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19686" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19687" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19387" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19691" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19682" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19692" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19694" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="19696" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19697" href="Algebras.Products.html#4023" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="19699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19700" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19702" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19221" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19703" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19705" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19682" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19706" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="19710" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19672" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="19716" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19716" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19718" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19720" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1826" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="19728" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19729" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1648" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="19735" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2841" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="19745" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19747" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1648" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="19753" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2841" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="19763" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

So, since `PS⊆SP`, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class `𝒦` belongs to `SP(𝒦)`.
